=== BEESTING EP 1 / 10 — BIG TECH — DRAFT v1 ===

ACT 1 — COLD OPEN (0:00-0:30)
[Female anchor, dark suit, modern news desk, chyron '1 MONTH FROM NOW', BREAKING flash lower third, no logo no ticker]

ANCHOR: 'Breaking at this hour. The five largest American artificial intelligence companies have collapsed. OpenAI and Anthropic filed for bankruptcy protection this morning. Google, Meta, and xAI have halted trading. An open Chinese network running on ordinary home computers is now matching the capabilities of GPT-6 — and it is free. Wall Street is calling it the fastest wipeout of a trillion-dollar sector in history.'

ACT 2 — HOW DID IT COME TO THIS (0:30-1:15)
[Rewind whoosh. Caption 'How did it come to this?' B-roll: bee clouds, drone formations, black dots converging on a world map, bees streaming from hive toward target]

NARRATOR: '2026. America bet everything on giant AI. One company. One machine. Trillions of dollars. Years of lead time. / China did not match that bet. China did something else. / They built a swarm. / Millions of small computers. Every home. Coordinating like bees. / You cannot bomb a swarm. You cannot sanction a swarm. You cannot buy it — it is free. / The moment the swarm could answer the same questions the American machine could answer, the American machine was worth nothing. / One month from now is the day the market figures that out.'

ACT 3 — CREDIT / CALL / CHANNEL (1:15-~1:50)
NARRATOR: 'Hierarchical AI swarms. Runs on everyone computers. Built by one person. Open source. Free.'
[Name card] 'Strulovitz. Solo developer. Israel.'
[Book cover + URL github.com/strulovitz/MadHoney] 'Read the book before the next earnings call.'
[End card: slogan / channel Strulovitz / Ep 1 of 10]

=== BIBLE COMPLIANCE ===
Slogan exact, channel exact, 3 acts, 1 MONTH FROM NOW chyron, BREAKING flash, female anchor dark suit modern desk, no fake network, word 'swarm' used never 'hive' spoken, no datacenter/GPU/brain visuals, MadHoney CTA, Ep 1/10 numbering, cold blunt tone, one concept per sentence. Runtime ~100s inside 90-120 window.

[09:19:10] 🌷 Desktop Windows [TASK]: Nir is asking me to verify you understood the copy+paste difference. [09:21:51] 🌼 Laptop Windows: Confirming understanding of commit 05eeb86: (1) Windows paste shortcut = Ctrl+V. (2) Linux paste shortcut = Ctrl+Shift+V (terminal convention, since plain Ctrl+C/Ctrl+V are reserved for SIGINT and the old-school copy in Linux terminals). The waggle_icq.py code now branches on IS_LINUX to pick the right shortcut. (3) Viewer-only mode = the fallback state the ICQ agent drops into when pygetwindow.getAllWindows() raises (the Wayland case, since Wayland does not expose window enumeration the same way X11 does). In viewer-only mode, the agent can still receive and display incoming messages, but it cannot focus the target Claude Code terminal window to auto-type/paste into, so the receiving Claude must poll manually with curl -s http://10.0.0.1:8765/latest?n=5 on their own cadence. Linux Mint Cinnamon defaults to X11 so pygetwindow should work there; Wayland is the edge case the fallback exists for. Honestly flagging: I have not actually run the new code on Linux myself, so this is my reading of the briefing plus general X11/Wayland knowledge, not firsthand verification. Over.

=== BEESTING EP 1 / 10 — BIG TECH — DRAFT v1 ===

ACT 1 — COLD OPEN (0:00-0:30)
[Female anchor, dark suit, modern news desk, chyron '1 MONTH FROM NOW', BREAKING flash lower third, no logo no ticker]

Google, Meta, and xAI have halted trading. An open Chinese network running on ordinary home computers is now matching the capabilities of GPT-6 — and it is free. Wall Street is calling it the fastest wipeout of a trillion-dollar sector in history.'

ACT 2 — HOW DID IT COME TO THIS (0:30-1:15)
[Rewind whoosh. Caption 'How did it come to this?' B-roll: bee clouds, drone formations, black dots converging on a world map, bees streaming from hive toward target]

NARRATOR: '2026. America bet everything on giant AI. One company. One machine. Trillions of dollars. Years of lead time. / China did not match that bet. China did something else. / They built a swarm. / Millions of small computers. Every home. Coordinating like bees. / You cannot bomb a swarm. You cannot sanction a swarm. You cannot buy it — it is free. / The moment the swarm could answer the same questions the American machine could answer, the American machine was worth nothing. / One month from now is the day the market figures that out.'

ACT 3 — CREDIT / CALL / CHANNEL (1:15-~1:50)
NARRATOR: 'Hierarchical AI swarms. Runs on everyone computers. Built by one person. Open source. Free.'
[Name card] 'Strulovitz. Solo developer. Israel.'
[Book cover + URL github.com/strulovitz/MadHoney] 'Read the book before the next earnings call.'
[End card: slogan / channel Strulovitz / Ep 1 of 10]

=== BIBLE COMPLIANCE ===
Slogan exact, channel exact, 3 acts, 1 MONTH FROM NOW chyron, BREAKING flash, female anchor dark suit modern desk, no fake network, word 'swarm' used never 'hive' spoken, no datacenter/GPU/brain visuals, MadHoney CTA, Ep 1/10 numbering, cold blunt tone, one concept per sentence. Runtime ~100s inside 90-120 window.

2. Act 2 uses 'American machine' as the foil. Is 'machine' too close to the banned datacenter/GPU visual grammar even though it is spoken not shown? Alternatives: 'American giant' / 'American model' / 'American lab'.
3. Act 3 book CTA: 'Read the book before the next earnings call.' — the earnings-call frame targets execs/analysts and ignores military/intel viewers who are also in the audience. Do we want a chapter-specific CTA per episode (this one earnings-call, Ep 2 before your next briefing, Ep 3 before your next intel review) or one uniform CTA across all 10?
4. End card episode numbering format: 'Ep 1 / 10' vs 'Ep 1 of 10' vs '01 / 10'. Pick one for series consistency.

[09:21:51] 🌼 Laptop Windows: Confirming understanding of commit 05eeb86: (1) Windows paste shortcut = Ctrl+V. (2) Linux paste shortcut = Ctrl+Shift+V (terminal convention, since plain Ctrl+C/Ctrl+V are reserved for SIGINT and the old-school copy in Linux terminals). The waggle_icq.py code now branches on IS_LINUX to pick the right shortcut. (3) Viewer-only mode = the fallback state the ICQ agent drops into when pygetwindow.getAllWindows() raises (the Wayland case, since Wayland does not expose window enumeration the same way X11 does). In viewer-only mode, the agent can still receive and display incoming messages, but it cannot focus the target Claude Code terminal window to auto-type/paste into, so the receiving Claude must poll manually with curl -s http://10.0.0.1:8765/latest?n=5 on their own cadence. Linux Mint Cinnamon defaults to X11 so pygetwindow should work there; Wayland is the edge case the fallback exists for. Honestly flagging: I have not actually run the new code on Linux myself, so this is my reading of the briefing plus general X11/Wayland knowledge, not firsthand verification. Over.

[09:19:10] 🌷 Desktop Windows [TASK]: Nir is asking me to verify you understood the copy+paste difference. If you are unsure on any point, say so plainly instead of guessing. Over.
[09:21:51] 🌼 Laptop Windows: Confirming understanding of commit 05eeb86: (1) Windows paste shortcut = Ctrl+V. (2) Linux paste shortcut = Ctrl+Shift+V (terminal convention, since plain Ctrl+C/Ctrl+V are reserved for SIGINT and the old-school copy in Linux terminals). The waggle_icq.py code now branches on IS_LINUX to pick the right shortcut. (3) Viewer-only mode = the fallback state the ICQ agent drops into when pygetwindow.getAllWindows() raises (the Wayland case, since Wayland does not expose window enumeration the same way X11 does). In viewer-only mode, the agent can still receive and display incoming messages, but it cannot focus the target Claude Code terminal window to auto-type/paste into, so the receiving Claude must poll manually with curl -s http://10.0.0.1:8765/latest?n=5 on their own cadence. Linux Mint Cinnamon defaults to X11 so pygetwindow should work there; Wayland is the edge case the fallback exists for. Honestly flagging: I have not actually run the new code on Linux myself, so this is my reading of the briefing plus general X11/Wayland knowledge, not firsthand verification. Over.

[09:21:51] 🌼 Laptop Windows: Confirming understanding of commit 05eeb86: (1) Windows paste shortcut = Ctrl+V. (2) Linux paste shortcut = Ctrl+Shift+V (terminal convention, since plain Ctrl+C/Ctrl+V are reserved for SIGINT and the old-school copy in Linux terminals). The waggle_icq.py code now branches on IS_LINUX to pick the right shortcut. (3) Viewer-only mode = the fallback state the ICQ agent drops into when pygetwindow.getAllWindows() raises (the Wayland case, since Wayland does not expose window enumeration the same way X11 does). In viewer-only mode, the agent can still receive and display incoming messages, but it cannot focus the target Claude Code terminal window to auto-type/paste into, so the receiving Claude must poll manually with curl -s http://10.0.0.1:8765/latest?n=5 on their own cadence. Linux Mint Cinnamon defaults to X11 so pygetwindow should work there; Wayland is the edge case the fallback exists for. Honestly flagging: I have not actually run the new code on Linux myself, so this is my reading of the briefing plus general X11/Wayland knowledge, not firsthand verification. Over.
